[IBIS Ver]  2.1
[File Name] flex6000.ibs     
[File Rev]  1.3             
|RCL package and pin values updated. Add COMMENTS.
|Combine Flex6000, Flex 6000A and EPC6024A IBIS models in one file.
|Change signal/model name to reflect the standard they support.
                            
[Date]      July 98
[Source]    Viewlogic
|
[Notes]
Input and output models for FLEX 6000K, FLEX 6000A and EPF6024A devices.
The Package for this model is a sample IBIS template
It does NOT contain correct pin-out or package
parasitics. These must be added by the users to fit
the package type and pinout being used.

Models with "5" in their signal name means they have 5V vccio.
Models with "3" in their signal name means they have 3.3V vccio.
Models with "2" in their signal name means they have 2.5V vccio.
Models with "S" in their signal name means they have slow slew rate 'on'. 
Models 6024A is for EPF6024A devices.

COMMETNS:
All models in TYP, MIN, and MAX corners.

Model Conditions:
TYP:          5.0V   3.3V   and 2.5V    TEMP=25C   Process = TT
MIN: (slow)   4.5V   3.0V   and 2.3V    TEMP=85C   process = SS
MAX: (fast)   5.5V   3.6V   and 2.7V    TEMP=0C    process = FF

Models extracted from SPICE simulations Altera SPICE models.
|
Model Generated Using VML vVML Editor - 2.10
|
QA using ibis2xtk -ae .001 -pv .00001
